0	AUTO	LOAD_TIP_044	Top Speed Challenge is about posting the highest speeds at each checkpoint along the race. Every checkpoint registers your top speed the moment you pass through it. The driver with the highest cumulative speed through all checkpoints wins the event.
0	AUTO	LOAD_TIP_045	Drag Racing is a competition between drivers to post the fastest drag time. In a Drag Tournament each driver gets 3 chances to post the fastest time. Staging well before each run and timing your shifts is the key to success.

0	AUTO	LOAD_TIP_047	In Drift Tournaments each opponent will take turns drifting on a course. Every driver will be scored based on speed, angle and how long they can hold a continuous drift.
